                                              Clean, quiet peaceful home
Beautiful rainforest garden where you can relax
10-15 mins drive to Cairns CBD

Reiki courses

                                            <div data-reactid="471">
                                              Welcome!

The House

This is a clean, quiet and relaxed home with a lovely ambience.  Spacious rooms and a large deck overlook a beautiful rainforest garden and there is a hammock and lounge to relax on.  

The house is situated in a safe, well established neighbourhood on the southside of Cairns 10-15 mins drive from Cairns CBD and Marina.  There is also a bus stop 7 mins walk away with buses available to the city.  The driveway provides off road parking for hire cars.  There is also a good 30 minute walk up the hill for those that would like some exercise in the morning - you can see Green Island from the top!  

The house has 2 spacious bedrooms, an open plan lounge area, one toilet and a separate bathroom.  The bedrooms have arched doorways and are separated from the main area by thick curtains.  Each room has a very comfortable queensize bed and sleeps 2.  

A large fully equipped kitchen with electric oven, gas top, microwave, Nespresso coffee machine and fridge is available for guests to use.  Most guests like to eat outside on the verandah overlooking the rainforest garden.  A bbq/grill is also available.  


This home is unique, surrounded by tall, magnificent trees.  Birds and butterflies are abundant here.  It makes a great base for those wanting to explore the Tablelands, Cape Tribulation and beaches.   Birdwatchers will also love the variety of birds here.

Free highspeed NBN wifi included &amp;  towels &amp; linen.

Tours &amp; Reef Trips

I love hosting people and am happy to help you plan your trip. For years I worked in travel in Cairns so can give you advice on where to go and where to get discounts on trips.  I also provide guided tours to Cape Tribulation or the Tablelands, etc if you are interested.

Reiki, Yoga &amp; Meditation

I facilitate reiki treatments &amp; teach Traditional Japanese Reiki here so if you are interested in learning please let me know.  Recently I completed my Yoga Teacher training so offer FREE yoga and meditation for those who are interested .

Breakfast Included

Continental breakfast is included..  Tea, coffee, muesli, toast, jam etc.

Please contact me for bookings and further information.  Julie

                                        <div class="listingDescription_1woxt0o" data-reactid="607">
                                          <div data-reactid="608">
                                            <div data-reactid="609">
                                              My fully renovated ‘Miners Cottage’ is a clean, spacious and beautiful home surrounded by tropical greenery.  It’s a welcoming place with a warm and relaxing atmosphere.  The common areas have exotic décor and there are many discrete places to relax.  My home is an excellent base for touring Cairns and its lush surroundings.   The Cottage is the perfect place to come home to after an energetic and inspiring day discovering the wonders of the Great Barrier Reef and rainforest.
                                            </div>
                                            <div data-reactid="610">
                                              My home offers all the modern comforts of a fully air-conditioned home.  There is a single bedroom with split system AC, ceiling fan and plenty of hanging and storage space. You have a private bathroom with separate toilet; a roomy dining and sitting area with a fully equipped kitchen - complete with micro-wave and toaster oven; stove top; and dishwasher.  Wi-Fi, ceiling fans, a wonderful lounge area complete with flat screen TV and cable TV, a DVD player with a wide selection of movies.  You will be provided with quality bed linen, towels and toiletries. (If more than one visitor, please see my additional listing with queen size bedroom.)
At the rear of the property, nestled within the tropical garden, discover a spacious undercover gazebo which is ideally situated for alfresco dining, conversing, reading, relaxing and enjoying Cairns’ tropical climate.  Couple this with a magnificent spa pool for relaxation or exercise, and you will understand the true meaning of ‘Tropical Paradise’.  This historical home is perfect for couples, travellers, families with a teenage child, or business people.
                                            </div>
                                            <div data-reactid="611">
                                              My home is situated in a quirky neighbourhood ideally located to the Cairns CBD.  At one end of my street, turning left, there is a community garden and a cycle/walking path which leads directly to the CBD.  The CBD is only 30 mins walk; 5 mins by car; ($10-$12 by taxi).  Turning to the right the cycle/walking path will take you along the side of the Cairns Inlet tributaries, over bridges, through bush land and past the racecourse.  At the other end of my street is a fabulous coffee house which also provides a great selection of food. An amazing Thai restaurant is just 4 mins walk away.

Westcourt Shopping Centre, featuring over a dozen Direct Factory Outlet (DFO) shops, is 1.1km - 4 mins by car.  Cairns Central Shopping Centre is 2.2km from my home, with the Reef Fleet Marina just 3.3km away.  The Reef Fleet will take you to the Great Barrier Reef and many of the islands off the coast of Cairns.
                                            </div>
                                            <div data-reactid="612">
                                              <li data-reactid="613">
                                                <p data-reactid="614">
                                                  이곳은 시티에서 약간 거리가 있는곳이지만 주위에 콜스와 헝그리잭 등을 이용 할 수 있어요.   주인인 제니는 아주 적극적으로 의견을 들어주려 하고 말을 더듬거려도 끝까지 들어주며 저에게는 아주 좋은 인상으로 남았어요.  내부 풀장이나 샤워시설은 아주 깨끗했고 집 전체적인 분위기는 아주 이국적이에요    시티에서 택시타고 들어가는 가격은 대략 10불 내외였고 아침시간에 그냥 슬슬 걸어나가면 걸어다닐만 합니다.   백팩커 이신분들은 집 구하기 전에 며칠 머물곳으로 현지 백팩커를 이용하는것보다 이곳을 강추합니다:)

                                          <div data-reactid="1589">
                                            <div data-reactid="1590">
                                              I live in an old Queenslander from 1939. Perfectly built for the tropical climate it would have seen many changes over the years. My yard is full of tropical food plants, I bet I'll introduce you to a plant you've never eaten before!
                                            </div>
                                            <div data-reactid="1591">
                                              I would like to share my home with you, a gorgeous tropical Queenslander (traditional wooden house) with a permaculture yard close to town. 
The house is located in Bungalow, which is only a 10 minute walk to town (Cairns Central). As public transport is not very good in Cairns you will enjoy this short walk, but you can also use one of my bikes to get around.
The house has 2 bedrooms, one bathroom, a dining room, a living room and a beautiful front deck on which you will definitely enjoy hanging out! 
The available room has a huge inbuilt wardrobe. it also has a ceiling fan and aircon and all windows in the house have mosquito screens, which is a must in the tropics. the bed is a sofa bed that sleeps 2 people, but has a thick mattress on a slatted frame (see pics). 
My backyard is an established permaculture food yard. This means that there are always yummy tropical plants and fruit available (like paw paw, passion fruit, bananas, kasava, lemons, oranges and others depending on the season) and the variety of plants attracts loads of animals like birds, butterflies, stick insects, lizards and frogs. But they all remain in the yard so don't fear them!
I have lived in Cairns for more than 7 years now, and the fact that I once came here as a tourist myself means that will be able to point you to the best tourist attractions but also the hidden treasures, that only locals know. Moreover I will be able to point you to the best bars, cafes and restaurants in town.
                                            </div>
                                            <div data-reactid="1592">
                                              Close to town. More info on best restaurants and coffee shops provided when you get here. There are heaps of places to choose from.

                                            <!-- react-text: 1721 -->                                            <!-- /react-text -->                                            <div data-reactid="1722">
                                              Surrounded by tropical gardens the home has 3 bedrooms (two for guests), a large deck that opens onto a swimming pool. Located in the quiet country town of Gordonvale which is just over 20 mins by car to Cairns, the gateway to the great Barrier Reef north and approx. 30 mins West to the Tableland where the Crater lakes, Cathedral fig trees and rainforest attract many visitors. 20 mins South there are sites such as 'Josephine Falls' and 'the Boulders'....and then further south Mission Beach.
Gordonvale is a small village with local bakery, Supermarket, butchers etc. The nearby Pyramid makes for an interesting climb with a great view for those who like trekking. 
Buses run on the hour. 
The 2 available rooms each have a Queen size bed.
I have many guests and enjoy experiencing people from other cultures, sharing meals and conversation.
